sVabout_me
p3140
V/\u000aSweet harmonies don\u2019t exclude noisy drones. Musical styles don\u2019t matter, if it comes to the point when excitation, tension or even silence is created within compositions. My focus of interest is in the soul of music.\u000aBecause human beings tend to be guided (and sometimes also faked) by bits and pieces of musical expressions which are constantly invading their brains, hearts and souls, i decided in a harsh and lonely winternight of 2005 to manipulate with soundscapes, reconstruct fieldrecordings and fool around with synth- and drum-modules for the rest of my life in search of sonorical wonderland.\u000agrounded and spiraled out. the journey continues.\u000ahttp://www.myspace.com/oscorlortormusork\u000ahttp://www.soundcloud.com/ambientanimal\u000ahttp://www.soundcloud.com/themerdepeople\u000a\u000a//\u000aBeside his sound-design/composition/production work benedikt guschlbauer is - together with clemens hausch and gerald krist! - also responsible for the monthly klub moozak event series held in vienna's fluc (http://www.fluc.at) and the moozak label specialised in experimental music and it's diversive sub-genres. The moozak label aims at sounding the boundaries of musical expression.\u000ahttp://www.moozak.org\u000ahttp://www.soundcloud.com/moozak\u000ahttp://www.myspace.com/klubmoozak\u000ahttp://www.flickr.com/klubmoozak\u000a\u000a///\u000aIn the summer of 2007 two musical maniacs combined their energies to form "restless ear syndrome", a dance-freakout-extravaganza-project which sees ambient animal (benedikt guschlbauer) and the freaky pocket (daniel friedl) tweaking the knobs and arranging the patterns in live-situations.\u000ahttp://www.myspace.com/restlessearsyndrom\u000ahttp://www.amiestreet.com/restlessearsyndrome\u000ahttp://www.amiestreet.com/restlessearsyndrome\u000a

sVbooks
p3639
Vtoo much to make a list of\u000a(or too little?)
p3640
sVabout_me
p3641
VI was born in a little town somewhere in Austria in the year 1983. My mother was a nurse and my father a Romanian immigrant who did almost every imaginable job for a while, from taxi driver to crane operator. From 1986 I was no longer allowed to play in the sandbox because of Chernobyl and my father's fear of all kinds of bacteria living in the dirt. In my early years, my best friend was TV and my first contact with the concept of digital image was a Commodore 64. In 1998, I attended a school for graphic design, which I finished successfully in 2003. Afterwards, I studied architecture in Graz in order to find out more about the possibilities of 3d animation and to extend my strategies for creating graphics and typography. In 2002, I started to make visuals for all kinds of electronic music. One of my hobbies is to collect strange examples of visual information on the internet, such as manuals of any kind, construction plans, fashion tablets and anatomic illustrations, and to combine them into new semantic chains and stories by means of video editing. Since 2005 I have been studying digital arts under Peter Weibel and Thomas Fürstner at the University of Applied Arts in Vienna. My points of interest are varied but all leading to a simple goal: to tell my own tales, in my own style, and to manifest my personal notion of the world using every available tool. 
p3642

sVabout_me
p3939
V\u000a24/7 is a musician duo/collective which suffers from multiple personality disorder. whereas one half/part of the duo/collective tries to lobotomize itself down to a single bass player, the other halfs/parts completely lost it over the years. after having parts of their personality in a bottled cloister in tibet fighting for its freedom the rest spread out to conquer the worlds eclectic music treasures. experiencing a 90 year old abbess as a teacher, the mind fragments mastered the 24/7 chambers of christian rap. recently the 24/7 held meetings at a betty fnord clinic franchise engaging all their personalities to form the worlds most underestimated new wave band. yesterday the plan was mutilated by two of the personalities - holding 51% of the shares - forcing the collective to attempt a master degree of obviously useless posing.\u000aenormous effort had to be made to pull out bloody contracts and sue the responsible fragments to hell. the product of this multiple split up expresses days going by, days going by - endlessly pulling you into the future. what did the florist say by the way?\u000alast saturday some of 24/7 was compiling new sound material. two thirds of the duo loved it and dropped in immediately to get rid of the recent explorations into advanced psycho shopping music. the remaining third kept its head stuck into a bag of audio cables causing the efficient set to head into a deflationsspiral. most of the tracks were hanged drawn and quartered - only one track of that material could be saved.\u000aone of the24seven split off the collective being hit by an acute schizophrenic episode and hid in a changing cabin of a turkish steam bath for 2 weeks pretending to be erdem tunakan. meeting Elvis residing in the neighbor cabin he was equipped with some digital drumsticks leading to the next brand new recording. its a love song about the late life of semi-herbivorous giraffes in the year of 2073.

NsVprofile_url
p6266
Vhttp://www.facebook.com/derivart
p6267
sVinterests
p6268
VOur work is located at the intersection between art, technology and finance. We conceive art as an exploration avenue to help us reflect and understand the social practices stemming from new technologies. Just as industrial production and mass media defined bureaucratic capitalism during the second half of the 20th C, we believe that the interactivity promoted by the computer revolution and new media are leading to new forms of social organization in contemporary times. We are interested in exploring those new organizational forms.\u000a\u000aIn the past three decades, the capital markets have been a leading adopter of digital interactivity. With the creation of electronic markets such as the Nasdaq in 1971 and Bloomberg terminals in 1981, Wall Street had its own Intranet two decades before other industries. Nowadays, electronic markets have replaced the traditional face-to-face exchanges in almost all of Europe. In this context, derivart examines social change at the beginning of the 21st C. by focussing on interactivity and new media in the capital markets. 
p6269
sVactivities
p6270
VDerivart explores the intersection of art, technology and finance. This art collective is comprised of a digital designer (Mar Canet), an artist (Jesús Rodriguez) and an economic sociologist (Daniel Beunza). Its projects include the curatorship of art exhibitions, production of art and the analysis of the capital markets.
p6271

p10322
g5
sVabout_me
p10323
VMatthias Tarasiewicz (a.k.a. parasew) is one of the founders of 5uper.net and CEO of the media prototyping company mutti.jp. Together with Georg Russegger and Michal Wlodkowski he is coordinating \u201cCoded Cultures \u2013 Exploring Creative Emergences\u201d. He was curating and producing over 100 Exhibitions and Art-related Events with 5uper.net (e.g. Coded Cultures \u2013 2004, Cuisine Digitale \u2013 2006, Playfulness \u2013 2008). While being active as a curator, artist and musician since 1998, Matthias is developing experimental media prototypes and researching in the fields of game theory, network theory and experimental media architectures. He studied visual Arts at the University of Applied Arts, Vienna.
